&lt;article class=&quot;markdown-body entry-content container-lg&quot; itemprop=&quot;text&quot;&gt;&lt;h1 dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;user-content-hello-world-with-java-coffee&quot; class=&quot;anchor&quot; aria-hidden=&quot;true&quot; href=&quot;#hello-world-with-java-coffee&quot;&gt;&lt;svg class=&quot;octicon octicon-link&quot; viewBox=&quot;0 0 16 16&quot; version=&quot;1.1&quot; width=&quot;16&quot; height=&quot;16&quot; aria-hidden=&quot;true&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill-rule=&quot;evenodd&quot; d=&quot;M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;&lt;/a&gt;Hello world with Java &lt;g-emoji class=&quot;g-emoji&quot; alias=&quot;coffee&quot; fallback-src=&quot;https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2615.png&quot;&gt;☕&lt;/g-emoji&gt;&lt;/h1&gt;
"><pre><code>    &lt;div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0"&gt;
&lt;article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"&gt;&lt;h1 dir="auto"&gt;&lt;a id="user-content-hello-world-with-java-coffee" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#hello-world-with-java-coffee"&gt;&lt;svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"&gt;&lt;path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;&lt;/a&gt;Hello world with Java &lt;g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="coffee" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2615.png"&gt;☕&lt;/g-emoji&gt;&lt;/h1&gt;
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This is a simple <strong>"Hello world"</strong> done with <strong>Java</strong> programming language.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-source-code" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#source-code"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><a id="user-content-source-code" href="#source-code"></a>Source code</h2>
<p dir="auto">This is the source code of the program:</p>
<div dir="auto"><pre><span>public</span> <span>class</span> <span>HelloWorld</span> {
  <span>public</span> <span>static</span> <span>void</span> <span>main</span>(<span>String</span>[] <span>args</span>) {
    <span>System</span><span>.</span>out<span>.</span>println(<span><span>"</span>Hello world!<span>"</span></span>);
  }
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Notice that <code>System.out.println("Hello world!");</code> shows the string <code>"Hello world!"</code> on the screen.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-compile-program" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#compile-program"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><a id="user-content-compile-program" href="#compile-program"></a>Compile program</h2>
<p dir="auto">To compile the "Hello World" program, type the following:</p>
<div dir="auto"><pre><span>javac HelloWorld.java</span></pre></div>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-excute-the-program" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#excute-the-program"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><a id="user-content-excute-the-program" href="#excute-the-program"></a>Excute the program</h2>
<p dir="auto">To execute the program, type this:</p>
<div dir="auto"><pre><span>java HelloWorld</span></pre></div>

  
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;/div&gt;
"><pre><code>&lt;/div&gt;
</code></pre></div>
  
  <details id="user-content-jumpto-line-details-dialog">
    <summary></summary>

  </details>
